	CLIENT CHARACTER VARYING(3) NOT NULL,
	PO_NBR BIGINT NOT NULL,
	VENDOR_ID BIGINT,
	STORE_NBR INTEGER,
	PURCH_GROUP_ID INTEGER NOT NULL,
	STO_TYPE CHARACTER VARYING(10),
	DELIVERY_DATE TIMESTAMP,
	EXE_SENT_DATE TIMESTAMP,
	TMS_SENT_DATE TIMESTAMP,
	TMS_PROCESSED BYTEINT NOT NULL
)
DISTRIBUTE ON RANDOM;

ALTER TABLE INFALOADER.ZTB_HOLIDAY_STO_PRE
ADD CONSTRAINT ZTB_HOLIDAY_STO_PRE_PK_IDX
PRIMARY KEY (CLIENT, PO_NBR);



CREATE TABLE INFALOADER.ZTB_LABEL_CHGS_PRE
(
	MANDT CHARACTER VARYING(3) NOT NULL,
	EFFECTIVE_DATE CHARACTER VARYING(8) NOT NULL,
	ARTICLE CHARACTER VARYING(18) NOT NULL,
	SITE CHARACTER VARYING(4) NOT NULL,
	POG_TYPE CHARACTER VARYING(1) NOT NULL,
	LABEL_SIZE CHARACTER VARYING(1) NOT NULL,
	LABEL_TYPE CHARACTER VARYING(1),
	EXP_LABEL_TYPE CHARACTER VARYING(1),
	SUPPRESS_IND CHARACTER VARYING(1),
	NUM_LABELS CHARACTER VARYING(2),
	CREATE_DATE CHARACTER VARYING(8),
	ENH_LBL_ID CHARACTER VARYING(2)
)
DISTRIBUTE ON (MANDT, EFFECTIVE_DATE, ARTICLE, SITE);

ALTER TABLE INFALOADER.ZTB_LABEL_CHGS_PRE
ADD CONSTRAINT ZTB_LABEL_CHGS_PRE_PK
PRIMARY KEY (MANDT, EFFECTIVE_DATE, ARTICLE, SITE, POG_TYPE, LABEL_SIZE);



CREATE TABLE INFALOADER.ZTB_ROLLOUT_USER_PRE
(
	MANDT CHARACTER VARYING(3) NOT NULL,
	USNAM CHARACTER VARYING(12) NOT NULL,
	ROLL_TYPE CHARACTER VARYING(5) NOT NULL,
	VENDOR CHARACTER VARYING(10) NOT NULL
)
DISTRIBUTE ON RANDOM;

ALTER TABLE INFALOADER.ZTB_ROLLOUT_USER_PRE
ADD CONSTRAINT ZTB_ROLLOUT_USER_PRE_PK_IDX
PRIMARY KEY (MANDT, USNAM, ROLL_TYPE, VENDOR);



CREATE TABLE INFALOADER.ZTB_SEL_DISCO_PRE
(
	SKU_NBR INTEGER NOT NULL,
	ZDISCO_SCHED_TYPE_ID CHARACTER VARYING(10),
	ZDISCO_MKDN_SCHED_ID CHARACTER VARYING(6),
	ZDISCO_PID_DT TIMESTAMP,
	ZDISCO_START_DT TIMESTAMP,
	ZDISCO_INIT_MKDN_DT TIMESTAMP,
	ZDISCO_DC_DT TIMESTAMP,
	ZDISCO_STR_DT TIMESTAMP,
	ZDISCO_STR_OWNRSHP_DT TIMESTAMP,
	ZDISCO_STR_WRT_OFF_DT TIMESTAMP
)
DISTRIBUTE ON (SKU_NBR);

ALTER TABLE INFALOADER.ZTB_SEL_DISCO_PRE
ADD CONSTRAINT ZTB_SEL_DISCO_PRE_PK_IDX_0521
PRIMARY KEY (SKU_NBR);
